But how can you do that using an Outcome quiz?&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In the Outcome quiz, you can\u2019t set up a variable and populate it with a value. BUT you can assign a tag to the results manually. Let\u2019s examine this with an outcome quiz I created regarding the scenario \u201cIs your website a lead generating machine?\u201d.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;I have three endings in this quiz&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;figure&gt;&lt;img alt=\&quot;\&quot; src=\&quot;https:\/\/uploads-eu-west-1.insided.com\/typeform-en\/attachment\/8fafb9b6-e810-443d-9751-8c288a24c09c.png\&quot; \/&gt;&lt;\/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Each ending has a separate call to action:&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;A will offer the users the opportunity to get some help building out their typeforms&lt;\/li&gt;\t&lt;li&gt;B offers the user to connect to a partner organization of mine to have a free analysis done on the website&lt;\/li&gt;\t&lt;li&gt;C provides a cheat sheet of information and actions the user can take on their website (upgrades typically required before having the analysis done in B or getting a custom typeform built)&lt;\/li&gt;&lt;\/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;What I really want to do is \u2018tag\u2019 the respondents and get that information into my CRM\/ESP for follow up sequences, contacting them, etc.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;But how can I do this with the Outcome quiz results?&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;I\u2019ve put all the details in a Google Doc that is available from &lt;a href=\&quot;https:\/\/typeformsolutions.com\/home\/outcome-quizzes-using-tags\/\&quot; target=\&quot;_blank\&quot; rel=\&quot;noreferrer noopener nofollow ugc\&quot;&gt;this blog post&lt;\/a&gt; - it\u2019s over 17 pages long so I did not want to put it all in this post in the Community.\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;There a link to &lt;a href=\&quot;https:\/\/www.loom.com\/share\/0aaccdecd2884c5b81a76e87c499bde0?sid=ffc1f3ba-e1ba-4219-b1e2-c5eba60324a2\&quot; target=\&quot;_blank\&quot; rel=\&quot;noreferrer noopener nofollow ugc\&quot;&gt;this video&lt;\/a&gt; in the Google Doc as well. It walks you through the process outlined in the Doc.\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hope this helps you figure out how to use \u2018tags\u2019 with Outcome quizzes.\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;cheers&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;des&lt;\/p&gt;&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:10716,&quot;featuredImage&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/uploads-eu-west-1.insided.com\/typeform-en\/attachment\/536080c5-7992-401a-8af2-bd391e626a19_thumb.png&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;member tips&quot;,&quot;replyCount&quot;:2,&quot;views&quot;:18,&quot;post&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:50216,&quot;author&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:93,&quot;url&quot;:&quot;\/members\/john-desborough-93&quot;,&quot;name&quot;:&quot;john.desborough&quot;,&quot;avatar&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/uploads-eu-west-1.insided.com\/typeform-en\/icon\/200x200\/e8d42515-af22-428a-afd1-f8b77119cbad.png&quot;,&quot;userTitle&quot;:&quot;Certified Partner &amp; Refer a friend, get rewarded (beta)&quot;,&quot;description&quot;:&quot;&lt;h3&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hello, Typeform Community! Know someone who could use Typeform? Now you can &lt;strong&gt;earn up to $500 by referring them&lt;\/strong&gt; \ud83c\udfc6&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;strong&gt;How does it work?\u2028&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;Just share your invite link to start referring.\u2028You can find this link by clicking on your account icon in the top right corner of the Typeform interface and choosing \u201cRefer friends, get rewards\u201d.&lt;\/li&gt;\t&lt;li&gt;When friends you refer sign up for a paid Typeform plan, you earn a reward.\u2028&lt;\/li&gt;\t&lt;li&gt;There\u2019s no limit to how many friends you can refer (the more, the merrier \ud83e\udd1d).&lt;br \/&gt;\t\u00a0&lt;\/li&gt;&lt;\/ul&gt;&lt;figure&gt;&lt;img alt=\&quot;\&quot; know it might be tricky to get to know all the possibilities you have when creating your Typeform\u00a0account. You may need more clarification on how to access the results to your form or how the forms collect data.\u00a0That\u2019s why we\u2019re here! &lt;img alt=\&quot;\ud83d\ude01\&quot; src=\&quot;https:\/\/cdn.jsdelivr.net\/emojione\/assets\/png\/1f601.png?v=2.2.7\&quot; \/&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To get started, here are some common questions related to this topic:&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Why is the timezone different when checking the export file vs the Results Panel?\u00a0&lt;\/em&gt;&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;content-spoiler&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:transparent;color:#000000;\&quot;&gt;We understand that you may see a difference between the submission time in your exported file and the Results Panel. &lt;\/span&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;\&quot;&gt;Typeform uses UTC (sometimes known as Z or Zulu) time in all of our integrations. The results section of your typefrom will use your browser\u2019s time to display the submission time, which is why you\u2019re seeing a difference between exported data and your account in terms of the date\/time stamp. Showing the submission time in UTC should help reduce any confusion If you\u2019re sharing the submission data with others across different timezones.&lt;\/span&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:transparent;color:#333333;\&quot;&gt; &lt;\/span&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:transparent;color:#000000;\&quot;&gt;\ud83d\ude0a&lt;\/span&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/content-spoiler&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Can I collect partial results if the respondent answers half of the form?&lt;\/em&gt;&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;content-spoiler&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:transparent;color:#000000;\&quot;&gt;Perfect timing to ask this question! \ud83d\ude0a &lt;\/span&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;\&quot;&gt;If the respondent doesn\u2019t click the &lt;strong&gt;submit&lt;\/strong&gt;\u00a0button, the responses won\u2019t be sent to your Results panel. However, w&lt;\/span&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:transparent;color:#000000;\&quot;&gt;e recently released a new feature so &lt;\/span&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;\&quot;&gt;respondents (as long as not using a private browser) are now able to partially complete, close and return to continue typeform submissions at a later date. You can learn more about this &lt;a href=\&quot;https:\/\/help.typeform.com\/hc\/en-us\/articles\/360029581051-Save-and-return-to-your-typeform-later\&quot; target=\&quot;_blank\&quot; rel=\&quot;nofollow noreferrer noopener\&quot;&gt;here&lt;\/a&gt;. This means any answers provided, even if the form wasn't fully submitted, will be saved in local storage for 15 days. When respondents return to your typeform, they will be taken to the start of the form, but will see their existing answers from their last visit. From there they will be able to review them and carry on to answer any remaining before submitting.\u00a0&lt;\/span&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;\&quot;&gt;*Remember, while data will be saved locally for the respondent, it will only appear and be stored in your Results after respondents click the final submit button.&lt;\/span&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;\/content-spoiler&gt;&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;img alt=\&quot;\u26a0\ufe0f\&quot; src=\&quot;https:\/\/cdn.jsdelivr.net\/emojione\/assets\/png\/26a0.png?v=2.2.7\&quot; \/&gt; If you have checked this post and the others from this category and still haven\u2019t found your answer, don\u2019t hesitate to hit the\u00a0&lt;a href=\&quot;https:\/\/community.typeform.com\/topic\/new\&quot; target=\&quot;_self\&quot; rel=\&quot;noreferrer\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;new post&lt;\/u&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;\u00a0button and start a new discussion.    username" style="color: ;" href="/members/liz-47">Liz</a></span><span class="user-title text--meta">Tech Community Advocate</span></div><a href="/your-typeform-results-32" class="topic-view_header-item text--meta"><span></span> <span class="topic-view_header-item_category-link">Your typeform results</span></a></div></div><div class="topic-view_info"><div class="topic-view_body-container"><div class="topic-view_body"><h4 class="thread-list-block__title"><a href="https://community.typeform.com/your-typeform-results-32/faq-your-typeform-results-137" class="qa-topic-title thread-list-block__title-link">FAQ: Your Typeform Results</a><span class="thread__content-type-pill pill pill--uppercase pill--article qa-content-type-pill">F.A.Q.</span></h4><p class="thread-list-block__content qa-topic-content"><a href="https://community.typeform.com/your-typeform-results-32/faq-your-typeform-results-137">We know it might be tricky to get to know all the possibilities you have when creating your Typeform account. You may need more clarification on how to access the results to your form or how the forms collect data. That’s why we’re here! To get started, here are some common questions related to this topic: Why is the timezone different when checking the export file vs the Results Panel? We understand that you may see a difference between the submission time in your exported file and the Results Panel. Typeform uses UTC (sometimes known as Z or Zulu) time in all of our integrations. The results section of your typefrom will use your browser’s time to display the submission time, which is why you’re seeing a difference between exported data and your account in terms of the date/time stamp. Showing the submission time in UTC should help reduce any confusion If you’re sharing the submission data with others across different timezones. 😊 Can I collect partial results if the respondent answ</a></p></div><div class="topic-view_footer"><button class="thread-meta-item thread-meta-item--hover-highlight thread-meta-item--likes qa-topic-meta-likes-icon" type="button"><i     if(document.querySelector('#register_is_invite') && document.querySelector('#register_is_invite').value) {
        let name = document.querySelector('#register_user_username');
        if (name.value === '--removed--') {
            name.value = ''
        }
        let email = document.querySelector('#register_user_email')
        email.readOnly = 1
        email.classList.add('register_user_email--disabled')
    }
</script>

<script src="https://public-assets.typeform.com/public/js-tracking/js-tracking-11.13.1.min.js"></script>

<script>
  (function ($) {

    const typeform_version = isMobile.any ? 'mobile' : 'v2'
    const attribution_user_id = jsTracking.attributionUtil.getUser()
    const category = 'public_site'
    const typeform_property = 'community'
    const insided_user_id = window.inSidedData.user.userid
    const COOKIE_USER_LOGGED_IN_FLAG = 'communityUserLoggedIn'
    const TYPEFORM_FUNCTIONALITY_BY_PATH_MAP = {
      '/typeform-updates-24/january-typeform-product-digest-8347': ['address', 'accessibility_checker', 'share_page', 'mailchimp-app']
    }

    function getTypeformFunctionalityForPath(path) {
      return TYPEFORM_FUNCTIONALITY_BY_PATH_MAP[path]
    }

    const convertToSnakeCase = (str) => str?.replaceAll('-', '_')

    function getCookie(name) {
      const value = `; ${document.cookie}`;
      const parts = value.split(`; ${name}=`);
      if (parts.length === 2) return parts.pop().split(';').shift();
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
      document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ";";
    }

    function deleteCookie(name) {
      document.cookie = name + '= ; expires = Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT'
    }

    const defaultProps = {
      typeform_version,
      attribution_user_id,
      category,
      typeform_property,
    }

    const tracking = {
      get mandatoryProperties() {
        return defaultProps
      },
      init() {
        if (jsTracking.consentUtil.hasFunctionalConsent()) {
          const options = {
            integrations: {
              All: true,
              Amplitude: jsTracking.consentUtil.hasPerformanceConsent(),
            },
          }

          jsTracking.client.init(
            '13PRPoCAmemn6i0qZSq8pnKYbRZ57rTB', // Dev key: N4DrQC6NYcQXbJZo6iAU2QLSymJGMQkI
            this.mandatoryProperties,
            options,
            'GTM-WH2ZQ3X'
          )
        }
      },
      trackViewPageSection: () => {
        const section = convertToSnakeCase($('.breadcrumb .breadcrumb-item.qa-breadcrumb-category a').attr('href')?.substring(1))

        const trackPageSectionProps = {
          ...defaultProps,
          section,
          page: document.location.href.split('?')[0],
        }

        const typeform_functionality = getTypeformFunctionalityForPath(document.location.pathname)

        if (typeform_functionality) {
          trackPageSectionProps.typeform_functionality = typeform_functionality
        }

        jsTracking.client.trackViewPageSection(trackPageSectionProps)
      },
      trackCreatePost: () => {
        jsTracking.client.trackItemClicked({
          ...defaultProps,
          item: 'create_post',
          item_type: 'button',
        })
      },
      trackLoggedIn: () => {
        const email = decodeURIComponent(getCookie('tf_email'))
        jsTracking.client.sendEvent('community_logged_in', {
          ...defaultProps,
          insided_user_id,
          email,
        })
      },
    }

    function initTracking() {
      if (!jsTracking.client.isEnabled() && jsTracking.consentUtil.hasFunctionalConsent()) {
        tracking.init()
        tracking.trackViewPageSection()

        /** Adding cookie to track whether the user has logged in or not, as there is no even to achieve that out of the box */
        const isUserLoggedIn = getCookie(COOKIE_USER_LOGGED_IN_FLAG)

        /** if the user is logged in and there is not flag in the cookie, create the cookie and track the event */
        if (window.inSidedData?.user?.userid && !isUserLoggedIn) {
          setCookie(COOKIE_USER_LOGGED_IN_FLAG, 'true')
          tracking.trackLoggedIn()
        }

        jsTracking.firstInteractionUtil.setFirstInteractionCookie()
      }
    }

    /** if the user is logged out, remove the cookie */
    if (!window.inSidedData?.user?.userid) {
      deleteCookie(COOKIE_USER_LOGGED_IN_FLAG)
    }

    initTracking()
    window.addEventListener(jsTracking.consentUtil.ONETRUST_EVENT, initTracking)

    $('.main-navigation--nav-buttons-wrapper a.menu-create-topic').click(() => {
      tracking.trackCreatePost()
    })

    const updatePlaceholderFunc = () => {
      const input = document.querySelector(
        'div.algolia-search-container input[type=search].search-box__input'
      )
      if (input) {
        input.placeholder = 'Search'
        clearInterval(updatePlaceholderInterval)
      }
    }

    const updatePlaceholderInterval = setInterval(updatePlaceholderFunc, 500)

    $('.btn--cta').click(function () {
      window.dataLayer.push({ event: 'cta_button' })
    })

    $('.main-menu-link').click(function () {
      window.dataLayer.push({ event: 'nav_element--main' })
    })

    $('.quicklink__url').click(function () {
      window.dataLayer.push({ event: 'nav_element--footer' })
    })
  })(jQuery)
</script>

<!-- END js-tracking -->

<link href="https://font.typeform.com/dist/font.css" media="all" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>
<link href="https://online-community.s3.amazonaws.com/public/styles/main.css?v=3" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" />

<script>
  /**
   * Utility functions
   */
   function isUserLoggedIn() {
    return !!window.inSidedData.user.userid;
  } 

  function isMobile() {
    return $(window).width() < 768;
  }
  
  function isUsernamePage() {
    // setUsernameForm page could be an error page if the user is not logged in
    return location.href.includes('setUsernameForm') && $('.twig_register-form').length
  }

  /**
   * Storage
   */

  const sessionStorage = window.sessionStorage
  const OPENED_ONCE_KEY = 'community-opened-login'
  const TIMER_KEY = 'community-login-timer'

  function setLoginOpened() {
    sessionStorage.setItem(OPENED_ONCE_KEY, 'true')
  }

  function wasLoginOpened () {
    return sessionStorage.getItem(OPENED_ONCE_KEY) === 'true';
  }

  function setTimer(currentSeconds) {
    sessionStorage.setItem(TIMER_KEY, currentSeconds.toString())
  }

  function getTimer() {
    sessionStorage.getItem(TIMER_KEY)
  }

  function clearTimer() {
    sessionStorage.removeItem(TIMER_KEY)
  }

  function getTimeLeft (currentSeconds, previousSeconds, maxSeconds) {
    return maxSeconds - (currentSeconds - previousSeconds)
  }

  /**
   * Modal functions
   */

  function showModal(modal) {
      app.events.commands.execute(`modal:${modal}:show`);
  }

  function showLoginModal() {
      showModal('login');
  }

  const LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_1 = { title: 'Welcome back', description: '' }
  const LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_2 = { title: 'Questions to ask? Wisdom to share?', description: 'Come on in...' }
  const LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_3 = { title: 'Got something to add?', description: 'Come on in...' }

  function setLoginModalVariant(variant) {
    $('#login-modal-title').text(variant.title);
    $('#login-modal-description').text(variant.description);
  }

  /**
   * Modal timer
   */
  function shouldDisplayModal() {
    return window.inSidedData && !isUserLoggedIn() && !wasLoginOpened();
  }

  function scheduleLoginModalTimer() {
    if (!shouldDisplayModal()) return

    const TIMER_INTERVAL_IN_SECONDS = 150
    const currentSeconds = new Date() / 1000

    let savedTimer = getTimer()

    if (!savedTimer) {
      setTimer(currentSeconds)
      savedTimer = new Date() / 1000
    }

    const timeLeft = getTimeLeft(currentSeconds, savedTimer, TIMER_INTERVAL_IN_SECONDS)
    
    setTimeout(() => {
      
      if (shouldDisplayModal()) {
        showLoginModal()
        setLoginModalVariant(isMobile() ? LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_3 : LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_2)
      }
      setLoginOpened()

      clearTimer()
    }, timeLeft * 1000)
  }

  /**
   * Modal Footer
   */
  const VIDEOASK_LOGIN_URL = 'https://typeform-sp-community.almostinsided.com/ssoproxy/login?ssoType=saml'
  const TYPEFORM_LOGIN_URL = 'https://typeform-sp-community.almostinsided.com/ssoproxy/login?ssoType=oauth2'
  const FOOTER_ID = 'modal_login-footer'

  const footer = `<div id="${FOOTER_ID}" class="login-modal-footer">
    <span class="login-modal-footer-emphasis">Don’t have an account?</span><br/>
    Sign up to <a href="${TYPEFORM_LOGIN_URL}">Typeform</a> or <a href="${VIDEOASK_LOGIN_URL}">VideoAsk</a> to join the community
  </div>`

  function appendFooterToLoginModal() {
    if(!$(`#${FOOTER_ID}`).length) {
      $('.qa-login-modal').append(footer)
    }
  }

  function sortModalButtons() {
    const button = $('.qa-login-modal .qa-sso-saml_v2').prop("outerHTML");
    $('.qa-login-modal .qa-sso-saml_v2').remove()
    $('.qa-login-modal .qa-sso-oauth2').after(button)
  }

  function bindButtonsToModal() {
    const createPostButton = $('.js-main-navigation ul li a').eq(0)
    const loginButton = $('.qa-header-login-button').eq(0)

    if (!isUserLoggedIn()) {
      loginButton.attr('href', '#')
      loginButton.on('click', () => {
        showLoginModal()
        setLoginModalVariant(LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_1)
      })
      
      createPostButton.attr('href', '#')
      createPostButton.on('click', () => {
        showLoginModal()
        setLoginModalVariant(isMobile() ? LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_3 : LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_2)
      })
    }
  }
  
  const usernamePageTerms = `I accept Typeform Community's <a href="/site/terms" target="_blank" class="terms">Terms and Conditions</a>`
  const usernameFieldDescription = `<span class="field-description">* Only letters, numbers, and spaces are permitted</span>`
  const usernamePageHeader = `
	<div class="username-page-header">
		<img class="username-page-image" src="https://public-assets.typeform.com/public/logo/wordmark_black.png" />
		<div class="username-page-community">Community</div>
	<div>`
  
  function updateUsernamePage() {
    if (isUsernamePage()) {
        $('.pagebox').prepend(usernamePageHeader).append('<div />')
        $('.termsLabel').html(usernamePageTerms)
      	$('.btn--cta').val('Join the community')
        $('.form__row:nth-last-of-type(5)').append(usernameFieldDescription)
      	$('.qa-page-title').text('Choose a username')
    }
  }
  
  function updateAskCommunityButton() {
    if(!isUserLoggedIn()){
      $('.btn--new-topic').attr('href', '#')
      $('.btn--new-topic').on('click', () => {
        showLoginModal()
        setLoginModalVariant(isMobile() ? LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_3 : LOGIN_MODAL_VARIANT_2)
      })
      $('.btn--new-topic').text('Join the community')
    }
  }
  
  function subscribeButtonRelocation() {
    $('.widget-container--product-updates_statistics_bar').eq(0).appendTo('.widget-container--product-updates_hero p')
  }

  updateUsernamePage()
  scheduleLoginModalTimer()
  appendFooterToLoginModal()
  sortModalButtons()
  bindButtonsToModal()
  updateAskCommunityButton()
  subscribeButtonRelocation()
</script>

<script>
function callback(mutationList, observer) {
  console.log("VIDEOASK");
  [].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('oembed'),function (el) { 
    
    // Bypass non videoask oembed elements
    if (!el.dataset.url.match('videoask.com')) return;
	
    // Remove the original iframe element
    el.firstChild.remove();
	
    // Create outer containers
    var div = document.createElement('div');
	div.className = "oembed-wrapper";
    
    var div1 = document.createElement('div');
	div1.className = "oembed-iframe-wrapper";
    
    // Create a new videoask iframe and append
    var url = el.dataset.url
    el.dataset.url = ''
    ifr = document.createElement('iframe'); 
    ifr.src = url; 
    ifr.width = '400px'; 
    ifr.height = '600px'; 
    ifr.allow='camera *; microphone *; autoplay *; encrypted-media *; fullscreen *; display-capture *;'; 
    ifr.border ='none';
    
    // Build the FE elements
    div.appendChild(ifr);
    div1.appendChild(div);
    el.appendChild(div1);
    
  })
 //observer.disconnect();

    console.log("ENDVIDEOASK");
}
  
callback();

const targetNode = document.querySelector("div.post") !== null;
const observerOptions = {
  //childList: true,
  //attributes: true,

  // 
  subtree: true
}

const observer = new MutationObserver(callback);
observer.observe(targetNode, observerOptions);

</script>
<!-- END VIDEOASK -->

<script>
$('.post__content a').each(function() {
   	var a = new RegExp('/' + window.location.host + '/');
   if (!a.test(this.href)) {
      $(this).attr("target","_blank");
   }
});
